In the Chinese restaurant and afternoon tea, the Chinese restaurant closes at 14:00. We came to the Chinese restaurant at 13:10, and were told by the front desk that they would not send numbers. What I saw was that the front desk had the final say on whether to send numbers (in fact, there were vacancies after two minutes, and other waiters also asked us to sit down). I think the front desk has too much authority. I think you should at least ask the manager whether to issue a number or not? To be honest, the food in the Chinese restaurant is also a matter of opinion. To be honest, there is nothing outstanding about it. There is no cost-effectiveness at all. It's just a dining environment (as shown in the picture, a warm reminder, 3 small crispy barbecue pork buns are 68 yuan). Overall satisfied, I will bring my mother to visit next time.
